//***************************************************************************

//*  Unit Item Tables
//*
//***************************************************************************

function Unit000070_DropItems takes nothing returns nothing
    local widget trigWidget= null
    local unit trigUnit= null
    local integer itemID= 0
    local boolean canDrop= true

    set trigWidget=bj_lastDyingWidget
    if ( trigWidget == null ) then
        set trigUnit=GetTriggerUnit()
    endif

    if ( trigUnit != null ) then
        set canDrop=not IsUnitHidden(trigUnit)
        if ( canDrop and GetChangingUnit() != null ) then
            set canDrop=( GetChangingUnitPrevOwner() == Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE) )
        endif
    endif

    if ( canDrop ) then
        // Item set 0
        call RandomDistReset()
        call RandomDistAddItem('I00C', 100)
        set itemID=RandomDistChoose()
        if ( trigUnit != null ) then
            call UnitDropItem(trigUnit, itemID)
        else
            call WidgetDropItem(trigWidget, itemID)
        endif

    endif

    set bj_lastDyingWidget=null
    call DestroyTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function CreateNeutralHostile takes nothing returns nothing
    local player p= Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE)
    local unit u
    local integer unitID
    local trigger t
    local real life

    set u=CreateUnit(p, 'nrvi', - 10595.5, 24500.5, 270.000)
    call SetUnitAcquireRange(u, 200.0)
    set u=CreateUnit(p, 'nrvs', - 10472.2, 24479.3, 270.000)
    call SetUnitAcquireRange(u, 200.0)
    set u=CreateUnit(p, 'nrvs', - 10713.5, 24554.8, 270.000)
    call SetUnitAcquireRange(u, 200.0)
    set u=CreateUnit(p, 'u010', - 19148.6, 25191.4, 300.760)
    call SetUnitAcquireRange(u, 200.0)
    call UnitAddItemToSlotById(u, 'I00C', 0)
    set t=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterUnitEvent(t, u, EVENT_UNIT_DEATH)
    call TriggerRegisterUnitEvent(t, u, EVENT_UNIT_CHANGE_OWNER)
    call TriggerAddAction(t, function Unit000070_DropItems)
    set u=CreateUnit(p, 'nssn', 25866.0, 6839.1, 271.452)
    call SetUnitAcquireRange(u, 200.0)
    set u=CreateUnit(p, 'nogl', 5208.8, 2590.7, 269.705)
    call SetUnitAcquireRange(u, 200.0)
    set u=CreateUnit(p, 'nogm', 5501.1, 2306.0, 262.686)

//===========================================================================
function CreateNeutralPassive takes nothing returns nothing
    local player p= Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE)
    local unit u
    local integer unitID

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Textes Flottants et Vision
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Textes_Flottants_et_Vision_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=0
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=11
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        call CreateFogModifierRectBJ(true, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], FOG_OF_WAR_VISIBLE, gg_rct_Zone_Initialisation)
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    // Se classe de haut en bas et de droite  gauche
    call CreateTextTagUnitBJ("TRIGSTR_7840", gg_unit_n00P_0046, 0, 9.00, 100, 100, 100, 0)
    // Kalimdor - 1re ligne
    call CreateTextTagUnitBJ("TRIGSTR_7812", gg_unit_n00P_0297, 0, 9.00, 100, 100, 100, 0)
    call CreateTextTagUnitBJ("TRIGSTR_7813", gg_unit_n00P_0298, 0, 9.00, 100, 100, 100, 0)

    // Royaumes de l'Est - 2e ligne
    call CreateTextTagUnitBJ("TRIGSTR_7819", gg_unit_n00P_0290, 0, 9.00, 100, 100, 100, 0)
    call CreateTextTagUnitBJ("TRIGSTR_7820", gg_unit_n00P_0291, 0, 9.00, 100, 100, 100, 0)

    // Northrend - 3e ligne

//===========================================================================
function Trig_Interdit_de_construire_Zone_Init_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( RectContainsUnit(gg_rct_Zone_Initialisation, GetTriggerUnit()) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Interdit_de_construire_Zone_Init_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call KillUnit(GetConstructingStructure())
endfunction

    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Interdit_de_construire_Zone_Init, function Trig_Interdit_de_construire_Zone_Init_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Reglages
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Reglages_Func024002002 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetUnitTypeId(GetFilterUnit()) == 'nbse' )
endfunction

function Trig_Reglages_Func025002 takes nothing returns nothing
    call SetUnitAnimation(GetEnumUnit(), "stand work")
endfunction

function Trig_Reglages_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call SetTimeOfDayScalePercentBJ(50.00)
    call FogMaskEnableOff()
    call StartTimerBJ(udg_Compteur_ConstructionRapide, false, 1200.00)
    call CreateTimerDialogBJ(udg_Compteur_ConstructionRapide, "TRIGSTR_7915")
    set udg_Fenetre_ConstructionRapide=GetLastCreatedTimerDialogBJ()
    call TimerDialogDisplayBJ(true, udg_Fenetre_ConstructionRapide)
    call SetForceAllianceStateBJ(GetPlayersByMapControl(MAP_CONTROL_USER), GetPlayersByMapControl(MAP_CONTROL_USER), bj_ALLIANCE_ALLIED_VISION)
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=0
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=11
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        call SetPlayerStateBJ(udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD, 100000)
        call SetPlayerStateBJ(udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER, 100000)
        call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('o02E', 24, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()])
        call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('n03H', 10, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()])
        call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('n03G', 10, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()])
        call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('n02N', 10, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()])
        call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('o039', 10, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()])
        call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('o03G', 10, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()])
        call SetPlayerAbilityAvailableBJ(false, 'A08G', udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()])
        call SetPlayerAbilityAvailableBJ(false, udg_CompetenceDonnerUnite[GetForLoopIndexA()], udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()])
        call CreateFogModifierRectBJ(true, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], FOG_OF_WAR_VISIBLE, gg_rct_R__gion_Spawner_et_heros)
        call SetCameraFieldForPlayer(udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], CAMERA_FIELD_TARGET_DISTANCE, 3000.00, 0)
        call UnitShareVisionBJ(true, gg_unit_n019_0371, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()])
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    call SetPlayerAbilityAvailableBJ(false, 'A08G', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE))
    call SetPlayerAbilityAvailableBJ(false, 'A08G', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE))
    call ConditionalTriggerExecute(gg_trg_Set_Admin_en_debut_de_partie)
    set udg_Lordearon=gg_unit_h003_0162
    call ShowUnitHide(gg_unit_h033_0275)
    call ShowDestructableBJ(false, gg_dest_DTsp_5091)
    call ShowDestructableBJ(false, gg_dest_DTsp_5092)
    call SetDestructableInvulnerableBJ(gg_dest_ZTd3_14859, true)
    call KillDestructable(gg_dest_LTt3_3178)
    call SetDoodadAnimationBJ("death alternate", 'D03R', 2000.00, GetUnitLoc(gg_unit_n00I_0397))
    call SetDoodadAnimationBJ("death alternate", 'D03R', 2000.00, GetUnitLoc(gg_unit_h0AH_0406))
    call SetDoodadAnimationBJ("death alternate", 'D03R', 2000.00, GetUnitLoc(gg_unit_n00I_0390))
    call SetDoodadAnimationBJ("death alternate", 'D03R', 3000.00, GetUnitLoc(gg_unit_n01F_0468))
    call SetDoodadAnimationBJ("death alternate", 'D03H', 1000.00, GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Interieur_Lordearon))
    call SetDoodadAnimationBJ("death alternate", 'D03R', 1000.00, GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Mont_Rochenoire_Interieur))
    set udg_GroupUnits=GetUnitsInRectMatching(gg_rct_R__gion_Spawner_et_heros, Condition(function Trig_Reglages_Func024002002))
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_GroupUnits, function Trig_Reglages_Func025002)
    call DestroyGroup(udg_GroupUnits)
    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("hide", 'YOtf', gg_rct_Campagne_Fleau_Lordearon)
    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("hide", 'YOfs', gg_rct_Campagne_Fleau_Lordearon)
    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("hide", 'YOtf', gg_rct_Campagne_Fleau_Dalaran)
    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("hide", 'YOfs', gg_rct_Campagne_Fleau_Dalaran)
    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("hide", 'YOtf', gg_rct_Campagne_Fleau_Village)
    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("hide", 'YOfs', gg_rct_Campagne_Fleau_Village)
    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("hide", 'YOtf', gg_rct_Campagne_Fleau_Bastion)
    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("hide", 'YOfs', gg_rct_Campagne_Fleau_Bastion)
    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("hide", 'YOtf', gg_rct_Campagne_Fleau_Stratholme)
    call SetDoodadAnimationRectBJ("hide", 'YOfs', gg_rct_Campagne_Fleau_Stratholme)
    call WaygateActivateBJ(false, gg_unit_n001_0362)
    // Lueur de hros dans Panthon
endfunction

function Trig_Reglages_commandes_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=0
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=11
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Commande_name, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], "-name ", false)
        call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Commande_couleur, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], "-couleur ", false)
        call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Commandes_passif_etc, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], "-passif", true)
        call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Commandes_passif_etc, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], "-hostile", true)
        call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Commandes_passif_etc, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], "-remove", true)
        call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Commandes_passif_etc, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], "-kill", true)
        call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Commandes_passif_etc, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], "-explode", true)
        call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Commandes_set_life_and_mana, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], "-set life ", false)
        call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Commandes_set_life_and_mana, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], "-set mana ", false)
        call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Commande_set_armor, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], "-set armor ", false)
        call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Commande_set_damage, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], "-set damage ", false)
        call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Commande_wood_and_gold, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], "-wood ", false)
        call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Commande_wood_and_gold, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], "-gold ", false)

        call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Commande_set_name_and_heroname, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], "-set heros name ", false)
        call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Commande_heros_level, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], "-set heros ", false)
        call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Commande_unite_couleur, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], "-unite ", false)

        call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Commande_effets_on_etc, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], "-content on", true)
        call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Commande_effets_on_etc, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], "-enerve on", true)
        call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Commande_effets_on_etc, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], "-tres enerve on", true)
        call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Commande_effets_on_etc, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], "-abandon on", true)
        call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Commande_effets_on_etc, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], "-heros on", true)
        call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Commande_effets_on_etc, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], "-feu on", true)
        call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Commande_effets_off_etc, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], "-tres content off", true)

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Set Admin en debut de partie
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Set_Admin_en_debut_de_partie_Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetPlayerSlotState(Player(11)) == PLAYER_SLOT_STATE_PLAYING ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetPlayerController(Player(11)) == MAP_CONTROL_USER ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Set_Admin_en_debut_de_partie_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Set_Admin_en_debut_de_partie_Func001C() ) then
        set udg_Admin=Player(0)
    else
        if ( Trig_Set_Admin_en_debut_de_partie_Func001Func001C() ) then
            set udg_Admin=Player(1)
        else
            if ( Trig_Set_Admin_en_debut_de_partie_Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                set udg_Admin=Player(2)
            else
                if ( Trig_Set_Admin_en_debut_de_partie_Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                    set udg_Admin=Player(3)
                else
                    if ( Trig_Set_Admin_en_debut_de_partie_Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                        set udg_Admin=Player(4)
                    else
                        if ( Trig_Set_Admin_en_debut_de_partie_Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                            set udg_Admin=Player(5)
                        else
                            if ( Trig_Set_Admin_en_debut_de_partie_Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                set udg_Admin=Player(6)
                            else
                                if ( Trig_Set_Admin_en_debut_de_partie_Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                    set udg_Admin=Player(7)
                                else
                                    if ( Trig_Set_Admin_en_debut_de_partie_Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                        set udg_Admin=Player(8)
                                    else
                                        if ( Trig_Set_Admin_en_debut_de_partie_Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                            set udg_Admin=Player(9)
                                        else
                                            if ( Trig_Set_Admin_en_debut_de_partie_Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                                set udg_Admin=Player(10)
                                            else
                                                if ( Trig_Set_Admin_en_debut_de_partie_Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
                                                    set udg_Admin=Player(11)
                                                else
                                                endif
                                            endif
                                        endif
                                    endif
                                endif
                            endif
                        endif
                    endif
                endif
            endif
        endif
    endif
    // -------------------------------
    call SetUnitOwner(gg_unit_h06M_0318, udg_Admin, true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerEventLeave(gg_trg_Admin_Leave, udg_Admin)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerEventDefeat(gg_trg_Admin_Leave, udg_Admin)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Appel_du_gardien, udg_Admin, "-Anti GM", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Fin_du_Gardien, udg_Admin, "-Fin du Gardien", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Fossoyeuse, udg_Admin, "-Fossoyeuse", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Lordearon, udg_Admin, "-Lordearon", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Changer_Admin, udg_Admin, "-set admin ", false)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Sauver, udg_Admin, "-sauver ", false)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Remove_un_joueur, udg_Admin, "-remove ", false)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Couleur_eau, udg_Admin, "-water ", false)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Musiques, udg_Admin, "-musique ", false)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Mode_zombie_on, udg_Admin, "-mode zombie on", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Mode_zombie_off, udg_Admin, "-mode zombie off", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Remove_un_joueur, udg_Admin, "-remove ", false)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Kick_un_joueur, udg_Admin, "-kick ", false)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Portes_des_Tenebres, udg_Admin, "-Porte Ouverte", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Portes_des_Tenebres, udg_Admin, "-Porte Ferme", true)
endfunction

    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Set_Admin_en_debut_de_partie, function Trig_Set_Admin_en_debut_de_partie_Actions)

                            if ( Trig_Admin_Leave_Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001Func001C() ) then

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Changer Admin
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Changer_Admin_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 1, 11) == "-set admin " ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Changer_Admin_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_Nombre=S2I(SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 12, 13))
    set udg_Admin=udg_Joueur[( udg_Nombre - 1 )]
    call SetUnitOwner(gg_unit_h06M_0318, udg_Admin, true)
    call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAll(), ( GetPlayerName(udg_Admin) + " est devenu Admin de la partie !" ))
    call TriggerExecute(gg_trg_Admin_Changer_Events)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Changer_Admin takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Changer_Admin=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Changer_Admin, Condition(function Trig_Changer_Admin_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Changer_Admin, function Trig_Changer_Admin_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Admin Changer Events
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Admin_Changer_Events_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerEventLeave(gg_trg_Admin_Leave, udg_Admin)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerEventDefeat(gg_trg_Admin_Leave, udg_Admin)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Appel_du_gardien, udg_Admin, "-Anti GM", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Fin_du_Gardien, udg_Admin, "-Fin du Gardien", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Fossoyeuse, udg_Admin, "-Fossoyeuse", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Lordearon, udg_Admin, "-Lordearon", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Changer_Admin, udg_Admin, "-set admin ", false)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Sauver, udg_Admin, "-sauver ", false)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Remove_un_joueur, udg_Admin, "-remove ", false)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Couleur_eau, udg_Admin, "-water ", false)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Musiques, udg_Admin, "-musique ", false)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Mode_zombie_on, udg_Admin, "-mode zombie on", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Mode_zombie_off, udg_Admin, "-mode zombie off", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Remove_un_joueur, udg_Admin, "-remove ", false)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Kick_un_joueur, udg_Admin, "-kick ", false)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Portes_des_Tenebres, udg_Admin, "-Porte Ouverte", true)
    call TriggerRegisterPlayerChatEvent(gg_trg_Portes_des_Tenebres, udg_Admin, "-Porte Ferme", true)
endfunction

function Trig_Tableau_Unites_Possedees_Func001002001001001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetPlayerController(GetFilterPlayer()) == MAP_CONTROL_USER )
endfunction

function Trig_Tableau_Unites_Possedees_Func001002001001002 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetPlayerSlotState(GetFilterPlayer()) == PLAYER_SLOT_STATE_PLAYING )
endfunction

function Trig_Tableau_Unites_Possedees_Func001002001001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return GetBooleanAnd((GetPlayerController(GetFilterPlayer()) == MAP_CONTROL_USER), (GetPlayerSlotState(GetFilterPlayer()) == PLAYER_SLOT_STATE_PLAYING)) // INLINED!!
endfunction

function Trig_Tableau_Unites_Possedees_Func008C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetPlayerSlotState(Player(0)) == PLAYER_SLOT_STATE_PLAYING ) ) then
        return false

function Trig_Tableau_Unites_Possedees_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_Counts_Players=CountPlayersInForceBJ(GetPlayersMatching(Condition(function Trig_Tableau_Unites_Possedees_Func001002001001)))
    call CreateMultiboardBJ(2, udg_Counts_Players, "TRIGSTR_7368")
    set udg_Tableau_Units=GetLastCreatedMultiboard()
    call MultiboardSetItemStyleBJ(GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 0, 0, true, false)
    call MultiboardSetItemColorBJ(GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 1, 0, 100, 80, 20, 0)
    call MultiboardSetItemWidthBJ(GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 1, 0, 12.00)
    call MultiboardSetItemWidthBJ(GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 2, 0, 4.00)
    if ( Trig_Tableau_Unites_Possedees_Func008C() ) then
        call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 1, 1, GetPlayerName(Player(0)))
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Tableau_Unites_Possedees_Func009C() ) then
        call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 1, 2, GetPlayerName(Player(1)))
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Tableau_Unites_Possedees_Func010C() ) then
        call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 1, 3, GetPlayerName(Player(2)))
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Tableau_Unites_Possedees_Func011C() ) then
        call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 1, 4, GetPlayerName(Player(3)))
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Tableau_Unites_Possedees_Func012C() ) then
        call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 1, 5, GetPlayerName(Player(4)))
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Tableau_Unites_Possedees_Func013C() ) then
        call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 1, 6, GetPlayerName(Player(5)))
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Tableau_Unites_Possedees_Func014C() ) then
        call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 1, 7, GetPlayerName(Player(6)))
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Tableau_Unites_Possedees_Func015C() ) then
        call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 1, 8, GetPlayerName(Player(7)))
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Tableau_Unites_Possedees_Func016C() ) then
        call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 1, 9, GetPlayerName(Player(8)))
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Tableau_Unites_Possedees_Func017C() ) then
        call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 1, 10, GetPlayerName(Player(9)))
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Tableau_Unites_Possedees_Func018C() ) then
        call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 1, 11, GetPlayerName(Player(10)))
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Tableau_Unites_Possedees_Func019C() ) then
        call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(GetLastCreatedMultiboard(), 1, 12, GetPlayerName(Player(11)))
    else
    endif
    call MultiboardDisplayBJ(true, GetLastCreatedMultiboard())
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Tableau_Unites_Possedees takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Tableau_Unites_Possedees=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventSingle(gg_trg_Tableau_Unites_Possedees, 2.00)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Tableau_Unites_Possedees, function Trig_Tableau_Unites_Possedees_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Actualisation du Tableau
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Actualisation_du_Tableau_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Tableau_Units, 2, 1, I2S(GetPlayerUnitCount(Player(0), false)))
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Tableau_Units, 2, 2, I2S(GetPlayerUnitCount(Player(1), false)))
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Tableau_Units, 2, 3, I2S(GetPlayerUnitCount(Player(2), false)))
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Tableau_Units, 2, 4, I2S(GetPlayerUnitCount(Player(3), false)))
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Tableau_Units, 2, 5, I2S(GetPlayerUnitCount(Player(4), false)))
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Tableau_Units, 2, 6, I2S(GetPlayerUnitCount(Player(5), false)))
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Tableau_Units, 2, 7, I2S(GetPlayerUnitCount(Player(6), false)))
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Tableau_Units, 2, 8, I2S(GetPlayerUnitCount(Player(7), false)))
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Tableau_Units, 2, 9, I2S(GetPlayerUnitCount(Player(8), false)))
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Tableau_Units, 2, 10, I2S(GetPlayerUnitCount(Player(9), false)))
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Tableau_Units, 2, 11, I2S(GetPlayerUnitCount(Player(10), false)))
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Tableau_Units, 2, 12, I2S(GetPlayerUnitCount(Player(11), false)))
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Tableau_Units, 1, 1, GetPlayerName(Player(0)))
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Tableau_Units, 1, 2, GetPlayerName(Player(1)))
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Tableau_Units, 1, 3, GetPlayerName(Player(2)))
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Tableau_Units, 1, 4, GetPlayerName(Player(3)))
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Tableau_Units, 1, 5, GetPlayerName(Player(4)))
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Tableau_Units, 1, 6, GetPlayerName(Player(5)))
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Tableau_Units, 1, 7, GetPlayerName(Player(6)))
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Tableau_Units, 1, 8, GetPlayerName(Player(7)))
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Tableau_Units, 1, 9, GetPlayerName(Player(8)))
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Tableau_Units, 1, 10, GetPlayerName(Player(9)))
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Tableau_Units, 1, 11, GetPlayerName(Player(10)))
    call MultiboardSetItemValueBJ(udg_Tableau_Units, 1, 12, GetPlayerName(Player(11)))
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Actualisation_du_Tableau takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Actualisation_du_Tableau=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Actualisation_du_Tableau, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_DEATH)
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Actualisation_du_Tableau, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_CHANGE_OWNER)
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Actualisation_du_Tableau, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SELL)
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Actualisation_du_Tableau, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SUMMON)
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Actualisation_du_Tableau, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_TRAIN_FINISH)
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Actualisation_du_Tableau, EVENT_PLAYER_HERO_REVIVE_FINISH)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Actualisation_du_Tableau, function Trig_Actualisation_du_Tableau_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Construction rapide
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Construction_rapide_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call TriggerSleepAction(0.30)
    call UnitSetConstructionProgress(GetConstructingStructure(), 80)
    call UnitSetUpgradeProgress(GetTriggerUnit(), 80)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Construction_rapide takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Construction_rapide=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Construction_rapide, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_CONSTRUCT_START)
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Construction_rapide, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_UPGRADE_START)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Construction_rapide, function Trig_Construction_rapide_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Construction rapide Fin
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Construction_rapide_Fin_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call DestroyTimerDialogBJ(udg_Fenetre_ConstructionRapide)
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Construction_rapide)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Construction_rapide_Fin takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Construction_rapide_Fin=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterTimerExpireEventBJ(gg_trg_Construction_rapide_Fin, udg_Compteur_ConstructionRapide)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Construction_rapide_Fin, function Trig_Construction_rapide_Fin_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Capitales
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Capitales_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_LIFE, GetTriggerUnit()) <= 500.00 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( UnitHasBuffBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'B00Y') == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Capitales_Func005C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetTriggerUnit() == gg_unit_h000_0037 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Capitales_Func006C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetTriggerUnit() == gg_unit_e00T_0020 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Capitales_Func007001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetTriggerUnit() == gg_unit_h0AH_0406 )
endfunction

function Trig_Capitales_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call SetUnitLifePercentBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 100)
    call SetUnitOwner(GetTriggerUnit(), GetOwningPlayer(GetAttacker()), true)
    call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAll(), ( "|cffff0000" + ( GetPlayerName(GetOwningPlayer(GetAttacker())) + ( "|r" + ( " a pris le contrle de " + ( "|cffffcc00" + ( GetUnitName(GetTriggerUnit()) + ( "|r !" ) ) ) ) ) ) ))
    call PlaySoundBJ(udg_sound02)
    if ( Trig_Capitales_Func005C() ) then
        call SetUnitOwner(gg_unit_h056_0158, GetOwningPlayer(GetAttacker()), true)
        call SetUnitOwner(gg_unit_h055_0064, GetOwningPlayer(GetAttacker()), true)
        call SetUnitOwner(gg_unit_h054_0065, GetOwningPlayer(GetAttacker()), true)
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Capitales_Func006C() ) then
        call SetUnitOwner(gg_unit_h06N_0398, GetOwningPlayer(GetAttacker()), true)
        call SetUnitOwner(gg_unit_h06N_0399, GetOwningPlayer(GetAttacker()), true)
        call SetUnitOwner(gg_unit_h06N_0401, GetOwningPlayer(GetAttacker()), true)
        call SetUnitOwner(gg_unit_h06N_0400, GetOwningPlayer(GetAttacker()), true)
    else
    endif
    if ( (GetTriggerUnit() == gg_unit_h0AH_0406) ) then // INLINED!!
        call SetUnitOwner(gg_unit_n01C_0408, GetOwningPlayer(GetAttacker()), true)
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Capitales takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Capitales=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Capitales, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_ATTACKED)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Capitales, Condition(function Trig_Capitales_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Capitales, function Trig_Capitales_Actions)
endfunction

function Trig_Rejoindre_une_faction_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('R01D', 0, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('R01C', 0, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('R01E', 0, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('R01G', 0, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('R01H', 0, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('R01I', 0, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('R01J', 0, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('R01K', 0, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('R01L', 0, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('R01M', 0, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('R01N', 0, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('R01O', 0, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('R01P', 0, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('R01Z', 0, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('R020', 0, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('R021', 0, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('R02L', 0, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('R02M', 0, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('R047', 0, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('R04L', 0, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    // Nouveautes de la faction
    if ( Trig_Rejoindre_une_faction_Func022C() ) then
        call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('R01U', 1, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('hkni', false, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('h02N', false, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('h09L', false, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('h02J', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('h02J', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('ndgt', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('Hant', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('H095', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Rejoindre_une_faction_Func023C() ) then
        call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('R01B', 1, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('R01Q', 1, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('R01R', 1, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('H05E', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Rejoindre_une_faction_Func024C() ) then
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('H0A6', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('u001', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Rejoindre_une_faction_Func025C() ) then
        call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('R01X', 1, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('O01T', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Rejoindre_une_faction_Func026C() ) then
        call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('R01W', 1, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('U00N', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Rejoindre_une_faction_Func027C() ) then
        call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('R01Y', 1, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('Ogld', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Rejoindre_une_faction_Func028C() ) then
        call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('R029', 1, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('R02A', 1, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('n021', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('Odrt', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Rejoindre_une_faction_Func029C() ) then
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('o01Y', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('n01U', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('n01Y', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('n01X', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('n01Z', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('O01Z', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Rejoindre_une_faction_Func030C() ) then
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('h05J', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('O01C', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('Ogrh', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Rejoindre_une_faction_Func031C() ) then
        call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('R01S', 1, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('R01T', 1, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('R04Z', 1, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('Hapm', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Rejoindre_une_faction_Func032C() ) then
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('H065', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('h030', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Rejoindre_une_faction_Func033C() ) then
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('O025', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('o01W', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Rejoindre_une_faction_Func034C() ) then
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('h06P', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('U00P', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Rejoindre_une_faction_Func035C() ) then
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('H04Z', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('u00Q', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Rejoindre_une_faction_Func036C() ) then
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('H04Y', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('o028', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('R050', 1, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Rejoindre_une_faction_Func037C() ) then
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('h008', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('R03V', 1, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('R048', 1, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('R049', 1, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('R04A', 1, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('R04B', 1, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Rejoindre_une_faction_Func038C() ) then
        call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('R04M', 1, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('R04N', 1, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('R04O', 1, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('R04Q', 1, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('R04R', 1, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('R04W', 1, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('R04X', 1, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerTechResearchedSwap('R04Y', 1, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('n087', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('n088', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('n089', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call SetPlayerUnitAvailableBJ('n08R', true, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    else
    endif
endfunction

    set gg_trg_Rejoindre_une_faction=CreateTrigger()

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Lueur de heros customs
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Lueur_de_heros_customs_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTrainedUnit()) == 'U006' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTrainedUnit()) == 'U011' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTrainedUnit()) == 'U01C' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTrainedUnit()) == 'H015' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTrainedUnit()) == 'E00X' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTrainedUnit()) == 'H08Z' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTrainedUnit()) == 'H08Q' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTrainedUnit()) == 'H08R' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTrainedUnit()) == 'H08S' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTrainedUnit()) == 'O00W' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTrainedUnit()) == 'O03C' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTrainedUnit()) == 'O03B' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTrainedUnit()) == 'H0C5' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Lueur_de_heros_customs_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not Trig_Lueur_de_heros_customs_Func001C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Lueur_de_heros_customs_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call AddSpecialEffectTargetUnitBJ("origin", GetTrainedUnit(), "war3mapImported\\GeneralHeroGlow.mdx")
    call SetUnitColor(GetTrainedUnit(), GetPlayerColor(GetOwningPlayer(GetTrainedUnit())))
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Lueur_de_heros_customs takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Lueur_de_heros_customs=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Lueur_de_heros_customs, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_TRAIN_FINISH)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Lueur_de_heros_customs, Condition(function Trig_Lueur_de_heros_customs_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Lueur_de_heros_customs, function Trig_Lueur_de_heros_customs_Actions)
endfunction

    return ( GetUnitTypeId(GetFilterUnit()) == 'h0BH' )

    return ( GetUnitTypeId(GetFilterUnit()) == 'h0BT' )
endfunction

function Trig_Effets_speciaux_Loop_2_secondes_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( CountUnitsInGroup(GetUnitsInRectMatching(GetPlayableMapRect(), Condition(function Trig_Effets_speciaux_Loop_2_secondes_Func001Func001001001002))) > 0 ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( CountUnitsInGroup(GetUnitsInRectMatching(GetPlayableMapRect(), Condition(function Trig_Effets_speciaux_Loop_2_secondes_Func001Func002001001002))) > 0 ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( CountUnitsInGroup(GetUnitsInRectMatching(GetPlayableMapRect(), Condition(function Trig_Effets_speciaux_Loop_2_secondes_Func001Func003001001002))) > 0 ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Effets_speciaux_Loop_2_secondes_Actions takes nothing returns nothing

    set udg_Colonne_Lumiere=GetUnitsOfTypeIdAll('h0BG')
    set udg_Eclair=GetUnitsOfTypeIdAll('h0BT')
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_Colonne_Lumiere, function Trig_Effets_speciaux_Loop_2_secondes_Func005A)
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_Aura_Malefique, function Trig_Effets_speciaux_Loop_2_secondes_Func006A)
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_Eclair, function Trig_Effets_speciaux_Loop_2_secondes_Func007A)
    call DestroyGroup(udg_Aura_Malefique)
    call DestroyGroup(udg_Eclair)
    call DestroyGroup(udg_Colonne_Lumiere)
endfunction

    call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A012', GetTriggerUnit())
    if ( (GetTriggerUnit() == gg_unit_h002_0254) ) then // INLINED!!
        call ModifyGateBJ(bj_GATEOPERATION_OPEN, gg_dest_B00R_15694)
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
    if ( (GetTriggerUnit() == gg_unit_h056_0158) ) then // INLINED!!
        call ModifyGateBJ(bj_GATEOPERATION_OPEN, gg_dest_B00B_5970)
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
    if ( (GetTriggerUnit() == gg_unit_h055_0064) ) then // INLINED!!
        call ModifyGateBJ(bj_GATEOPERATION_OPEN, gg_dest_B00C_6601)
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
    if ( (GetTriggerUnit() == gg_unit_h054_0065) ) then // INLINED!!
        call ModifyGateBJ(bj_GATEOPERATION_OPEN, gg_dest_B00C_1835)
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
    if ( (GetTriggerUnit() == gg_unit_h001_0221) ) then // INLINED!!
        call ModifyGateBJ(bj_GATEOPERATION_OPEN, gg_dest_B00E_1689)
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
    if ( (GetTriggerUnit() == udg_Lordearon) ) then // INLINED!!
        call ModifyGateBJ(bj_GATEOPERATION_OPEN, gg_dest_LTg1_6930)
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
    if ( (GetTriggerUnit() == gg_unit_h05V_0249) ) then // INLINED!!
        call ModifyGateBJ(bj_GATEOPERATION_OPEN, gg_dest_LTg1_6046)
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
    if ( (GetTriggerUnit() == gg_unit_h007_0235) ) then // INLINED!!
        call ModifyGateBJ(bj_GATEOPERATION_OPEN, gg_dest_DTg5_6932)
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
    if ( (GetTriggerUnit() == gg_unit_h005_0233) ) then // INLINED!!
        call ModifyGateBJ(bj_GATEOPERATION_OPEN, gg_dest_DTg8_6931)
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
    if ( (GetTriggerUnit() == gg_unit_h05F_0270) ) then // INLINED!!
        call ModifyGateBJ(bj_GATEOPERATION_OPEN, gg_dest_B00H_1686)
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
    if ( (GetTriggerUnit() == gg_unit_h05G_0271) ) then // INLINED!!
        call ModifyGateBJ(bj_GATEOPERATION_OPEN, gg_dest_YTcx_11976)
    else
        call DoNothing()

    if ( (GetTriggerUnit() == gg_unit_h0AH_0406) ) then // INLINED!!
        call ModifyGateBJ(bj_GATEOPERATION_OPEN, gg_dest_B00G_5094)

function Trig_Porte_de_Thoradin_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A04U' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Porte_de_Thoradin_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A05C' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Porte_de_Thoradin_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Porte_de_Thoradin_Func001C() ) then
        call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('A04U', GetTriggerUnit())
        call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A05C', GetTriggerUnit())
        call ModifyGateBJ(bj_GATEOPERATION_OPEN, gg_dest_B00N_9874)
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Porte_de_Thoradin_Func002C() ) then
        call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('A05C', GetTriggerUnit())
        call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A04U', GetTriggerUnit())
        call ModifyGateBJ(bj_GATEOPERATION_CLOSE, gg_dest_B00N_9874)
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Lever et Abaisser Pont de Thandol
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Lever_et_Abaisser_Pont_de_Thandol_Func001Func004002002 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( IsUnitType(GetFilterUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_FLYING) == false )
endfunction

function Trig_Lever_et_Abaisser_Pont_de_Thandol_Func001Func005002 takes nothing returns nothing
    call KillUnit(GetEnumUnit())
endfunction

function Trig_Lever_et_Abaisser_Pont_de_Thandol_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetTriggerUnit() == gg_unit_h052_0278 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A00Z' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Lever_et_Abaisser_Pont_de_Thandol_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetTriggerUnit() == gg_unit_h052_0278 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A010' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Lever_et_Abaisser_Pont_de_Thandol_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Lever_et_Abaisser_Pont_de_Thandol_Func001C() ) then
        call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('A00Z', GetTriggerUnit())
        call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A010', GetTriggerUnit())
        call KillDestructable(gg_dest_LT04_2365)
        set udg_GroupUnits=GetUnitsInRectMatching(gg_rct_Pont_de_Thandol, Condition(function Trig_Lever_et_Abaisser_Pont_de_Thandol_Func001Func004002002))
        call ForGroupBJ(udg_GroupUnits, function Trig_Lever_et_Abaisser_Pont_de_Thandol_Func001Func005002)
        call DestroyGroup(udg_GroupUnits)
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Lever_et_Abaisser_Pont_de_Thandol_Func002C() ) then
        call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('A010', GetTriggerUnit())
        call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A00Z', GetTriggerUnit())
        call DestructableRestoreLife(gg_dest_LT04_2365, GetDestructableMaxLife(gg_dest_LT04_2365), true)
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Lever_et_Abaisser_Pont_de_Thandol takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Lever_et_Abaisser_Pont_de_Thandol=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Lever_et_Abaisser_Pont_de_Thandol, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_EFFECT)

        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetTriggerUnit() == gg_unit_n01C_0408 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true

    return ( IsUnitType(GetFilterUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_FLYING) == false )
endfunction

    call KillUnit(GetEnumUnit())
endfunction

function Trig_Piege_Schomolance_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call ShowDestructableBJ(true, gg_dest_DTsp_5091)
    call ShowDestructableBJ(true, gg_dest_DTsp_5092)
    set udg_GroupUnits=GetUnitsInRectMatching(gg_rct_Piege_Epieux_Schomolance, Condition(function Trig_Piege_Schomolance_Func003002002))
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_GroupUnits, function Trig_Piege_Schomolance_Func004002)
    call DestroyGroup(udg_GroupUnits)
    call TriggerSleepAction(6.00)
    call ShowDestructableBJ(false, gg_dest_DTsp_5091)
    call ShowDestructableBJ(false, gg_dest_DTsp_5092)
endfunction

function Trig_Prisons_magiques_Dalaran_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call DestructableRestoreLife(GetDyingDestructable(), GetDestructableMaxLife(GetDyingDestructable()), true)
    if ( Trig_Prisons_magiques_Dalaran_Func002C() ) then
        if ( (IsDestructableAliveBJ(gg_dest_XTmp_2376) == true) ) then // INLINED!!
            call KillDestructable(gg_dest_XTmp_2376)
        else
            call DestructableRestoreLife(gg_dest_XTmp_2376, GetDestructableMaxLife(gg_dest_XTmp_2376), true)
        endif
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Prisons_magiques_Dalaran_Func003C() ) then
        if ( (IsDestructableAliveBJ(gg_dest_XTmp_2377) == true) ) then // INLINED!!
            call KillDestructable(gg_dest_XTmp_2377)
        else
            call DestructableRestoreLife(gg_dest_XTmp_2377, GetDestructableMaxLife(gg_dest_XTmp_2377), true)
        endif
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Prisons_magiques_Dalaran_Func004C() ) then
        if ( (IsDestructableAliveBJ(gg_dest_XTmp_2378) == true) ) then // INLINED!!
            call KillDestructable(gg_dest_XTmp_2378)
        else
            call DestructableRestoreLife(gg_dest_XTmp_2378, GetDestructableMaxLife(gg_dest_XTmp_2378), true)
        endif
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Prisons_magiques_Dalaran_Func005C() ) then
        if ( (IsDestructableAliveBJ(gg_dest_XTmp_2379) == true) ) then // INLINED!!
            call KillDestructable(gg_dest_XTmp_2379)
        else
            call DestructableRestoreLife(gg_dest_XTmp_2379, GetDestructableMaxLife(gg_dest_XTmp_2379), true)
        endif
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Anneau du Kirin Tor
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Anneau_du_Kirin_Tor_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetItemTypeId(GetManipulatedItem()) == 'I00P' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Anneau_du_Kirin_Tor_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( UnitHasItemOfTypeBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'I00F') == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( UnitHasItemOfTypeBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'I00E') == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( UnitHasItemOfTypeBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'I00D') == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( UnitHasItemOfTypeBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'I00C') == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Anneau_du_Kirin_Tor_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Anneau_du_Kirin_Tor_Func002C() ) then
        call RemoveItem(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'I00F'))
        call RemoveItem(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'I00E'))
        call RemoveItem(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'I00D'))
        call RemoveItem(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'I00C'))
        call RemoveItem(GetItemOfTypeFromUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'I00P'))
        call CreateItemLoc('I008', GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit()))
        call UnitAddItemSwapped(GetLastCreatedItem(), GetTriggerUnit())
        call AddSpecialEffectTargetUnitBJ("origin", GetTriggerUnit(), "Abilities\\Weapons\\Bolt\\BoltImpact.mdl")
        call UnitAddItemSwapped(GetLastCreatedItem(), GetTriggerUnit())
        call TriggerSleepAction(2.00)
        call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
        call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAll(), ( GetPlayerName(GetTriggerPlayer()) + " a forg l'|cffff0000Anneau du Kirin Tor !|r" ))
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Anneau_du_Kirin_Tor takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Anneau_du_Kirin_Tor=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Anneau_du_Kirin_Tor, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_PICKUP_ITEM)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Anneau_du_Kirin_Tor, Condition(function Trig_Anneau_du_Kirin_Tor_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Anneau_du_Kirin_Tor, function Trig_Anneau_du_Kirin_Tor_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Chopine de bierre
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Chopine_de_bierre_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetItemTypeId(GetManipulatedItem()) == 'I00R' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Chopine_de_bierre_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call CreateTextTagUnitBJ("TRIGSTR_6687", GetTriggerUnit(), 0, 9.00, 100, 0.00, 0.00, 0)
    call SetTextTagVelocityBJ(GetLastCreatedTextTag(), 64, 90)
    call SetTextTagPermanentBJ(GetLastCreatedTextTag(), false)
    call SetTextTagLifespanBJ(GetLastCreatedTextTag(), 4.00)
    call SetTextTagFadepointBJ(GetLastCreatedTextTag(), 2.00)
    set udg_Position=GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit())
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'h06L', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_Position, bj_UNIT_FACING)
    call UnitApplyTimedLifeBJ(3.00, 'BTLF', GetLastCreatedUnit())
    call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A05A', GetLastCreatedUnit())
    call IssueTargetOrderBJ(GetLastCreatedUnit(), "cripple", GetTriggerUnit())
    call RemoveLocation(udg_Position)
    set udg_Position=GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit())
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'h06L', Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), udg_Position, bj_UNIT_FACING)
    call UnitApplyTimedLifeBJ(3.00, 'BTLF', GetLastCreatedUnit())
    call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A059', GetLastCreatedUnit())
    call IssueTargetOrderBJ(GetLastCreatedUnit(), "curse", GetTriggerUnit())
    call RemoveLocation(udg_Position)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Chopine_de_bierre takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Chopine_de_bierre=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Chopine_de_bierre, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_USE_ITEM)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Chopine_de_bierre, Condition(function Trig_Chopine_de_bierre_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Chopine_de_bierre, function Trig_Chopine_de_bierre_Actions)
endfunction

function Trig_Campagne_Ile_de_Sargeras_Func002Func021002002 takes nothing returns boolean
    return GetBooleanAnd((GetOwningPlayer(GetFilterUnit()) == Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE)), (GetUnitRace(GetFilterUnit()) == RACE_ORC)) // INLINED!!
endfunction

function Trig_Campagne_Ile_de_Sargeras_Func002Func022002 takes nothing returns nothing
    call SetUnitOwner(GetEnumUnit(), Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), true)
endfunction

function Trig_Campagne_Ile_de_Sargeras_Func002Func024002002 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetOwningPlayer(GetFilterUnit()) == Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE) )
endfunction

function Trig_Campagne_Ile_de_Sargeras_Func002Func025Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetEnumUnit() != gg_unit_n094_0392 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetEnumUnit() != gg_unit_n00I_0253 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( GetEnumUnit() != gg_unit_n00H_0391 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Campagne_Ile_de_Sargeras_Func002Func025A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Campagne_Ile_de_Sargeras_Func002Func025Func001C() ) then
        call SetUnitOwner(GetEnumUnit(), GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), true)
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Campagne_Ile_de_Sargeras_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'Eevi' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Campagne_Ile_de_Sargeras_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Campagne_Ile_de_Sargeras_Func001C() ) then
        call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=0
        set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=11
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
            call SetPlayerAbilityAvailableBJ(false, 'A01H', udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()])
            set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
        endloop
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=0
        set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=11
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
            call SetPlayerAbilityAvailableBJ(false, 'A01I', udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()])
            set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
        endloop
        set udg_Position=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Ile_de_Sargeras_Exterieur)
        call SetUnitPositionLoc(GetTriggerUnit(), udg_Position)
        call PauseUnitBJ(true, GetTriggerUnit())
        call RemoveLocation(udg_Position)
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=0
        set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=5
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
            call SetUnitAnimation(GetTriggerUnit(), "spell")
            call AddSpecialEffectTargetUnitBJ("origin", GetTriggerUnit(), "Abilities\\Spells\\Other\\Charm\\CharmTarget.mdl")
            call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
            call TriggerSleepAction(1.00)
            set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
        endloop
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=0
        set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=11
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
            call CameraSetEQNoiseForPlayer(udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], 4.00)
            set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
        endloop
        call TriggerSleepAction(5.00)
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=0
        set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=11
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
            call CameraClearNoiseForPlayer(udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()])
            set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
        endloop
        call ShowUnitShow(gg_unit_n02I_0393)
        set udg_Position=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Ile_de_Sargeras_Exterieur)
        call PingMinimapLocForForce(GetPlayersAll(), udg_Position, 2.00)
        call RemoveLocation(udg_Position)
        call PlaySoundBJ(gg_snd_Hint)
        call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAll(), "TRIGSTR_7926")
        call PauseUnitBJ(false, GetTriggerUnit())
        call IssueTargetOrderBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), "smart", gg_unit_n02I_0393)
        call ForceCinematicSubtitlesBJ(true)
        call TransmissionFromUnitTypeWithNameBJ(GetPlayersAll(), GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), 'Ogld', "TRIGSTR_7924", GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit()), gg_snd_S03Guldan08, "TRIGSTR_7925", bj_TIMETYPE_ADD, 0, false)
        set udg_GroupUnits=GetUnitsInRectMatching(gg_rct_Ile_et_Tombe_de_Sargeras, Condition(function Trig_Campagne_Ile_de_Sargeras_Func001Func022002002))
        call ForGroupBJ(udg_GroupUnits, function Trig_Campagne_Ile_de_Sargeras_Func001Func023002)
        call DestroyGroup(udg_GroupUnits)
        set udg_GroupUnits=GetUnitsInRectMatching(gg_rct_Ile_et_Tombe_de_Sargeras, Condition(function Trig_Campagne_Ile_de_Sargeras_Func001Func025002002))
        call ForGroupBJ(udg_GroupUnits, function Trig_Campagne_Ile_de_Sargeras_Func001Func026A)
        call DestroyGroup(udg_GroupUnits)
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Campagne_Ile_de_Sargeras_Func002C() ) then
        call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=0
        set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=11
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
            call SetPlayerAbilityAvailableBJ(false, 'A01H', udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()])
            set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
        endloop
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=0
        set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=11
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
            call SetPlayerAbilityAvailableBJ(false, 'A01I', udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()])
            set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
        endloop
        set udg_Position=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Ile_de_Sargeras_Exterieur)
        call SetUnitPositionLoc(GetTriggerUnit(), udg_Position)
        call PauseUnitBJ(true, GetTriggerUnit())
        call RemoveLocation(udg_Position)
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=0
        set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=5
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
            call SetUnitAnimation(GetTriggerUnit(), "spell")
            call AddSpecialEffectTargetUnitBJ("origin", GetTriggerUnit(), "Abilities\\Spells\\Other\\Charm\\CharmTarget.mdl")
            call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
            call TriggerSleepAction(1.00)
            set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
        endloop
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=0
        set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=11
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
            call CameraSetEQNoiseForPlayer(udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], 4.00)
            set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
        endloop
        call TriggerSleepAction(5.00)
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=0
        set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=11
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
            call CameraClearNoiseForPlayer(udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()])
            set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
        endloop
        call ShowUnitShow(gg_unit_n02I_0393)
        set udg_Position=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Ile_de_Sargeras_Exterieur)
        call PingMinimapLocForForce(GetPlayersAll(), udg_Position, 2.00)
        call RemoveLocation(udg_Position)
        call PlaySoundBJ(gg_snd_Hint)
        call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAll(), "TRIGSTR_7927")
        call PauseUnitBJ(false, GetTriggerUnit())
        call IssueTargetOrderBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), "smart", gg_unit_n02I_0393)
        call TransmissionFromUnitTypeWithNameBJ(GetPlayersAll(), GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), 'Eevi', "TRIGSTR_7928", GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit()), gg_snd_S07Illidan30, "TRIGSTR_7929", bj_TIMETYPE_ADD, 0, false)
        set udg_GroupUnits=GetUnitsInRectMatching(gg_rct_Ile_et_Tombe_de_Sargeras, Condition(function Trig_Campagne_Ile_de_Sargeras_Func002Func021002002))
        call ForGroupBJ(udg_GroupUnits, function Trig_Campagne_Ile_de_Sargeras_Func002Func022002)
        call DestroyGroup(udg_GroupUnits)
        set udg_GroupUnits=GetUnitsInRectMatching(gg_rct_Ile_et_Tombe_de_Sargeras, Condition(function Trig_Campagne_Ile_de_Sargeras_Func002Func024002002))
        call ForGroupBJ(udg_GroupUnits, function Trig_Campagne_Ile_de_Sargeras_Func002Func025A)
        call DestroyGroup(udg_GroupUnits)
    else
    endif
endfunction

    set gg_trg_Campagne_Ile_de_Sargeras=CreateTrigger()

function Trig_Antre_de_Sargeras_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitInGroup(GetTriggerUnit(), GetUnitsInRectAll(gg_rct_Activer_Sargeras)) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Antre_de_Sargeras_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Antre_de_Sargeras_Func001C() ) then
        call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
        call TriggerSleepAction(1.00)
        call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Activer_Sargeras), "Doodads\\Cinematic\\TownBurningFireEmitter\\TownBurningFireEmitter.mdl")
        call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Activer_Sargeras), "Doodads\\Cinematic\\TownBurningFireEmitter\\TownBurningFireEmitter.mdl")
        call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Activer_Sargeras), "Doodads\\Cinematic\\TownBurningFireEmitter\\TownBurningFireEmitter.mdl")
        call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Activer_Sargeras), "Doodads\\Cinematic\\TownBurningFireEmitter\\TownBurningFireEmitter.mdl")
        call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Activer_Sargeras), "Doodads\\Cinematic\\TownBurningFireEmitter\\TownBurningFireEmitter.mdl")
        call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Activer_Sargeras), "Doodads\\Cinematic\\TownBurningFireEmitter\\TownBurningFireEmitter.mdl")
        call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Activer_Sargeras), "Doodads\\Cinematic\\TownBurningFireEmitter\\TownBurningFireEmitter.mdl")
        call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Activer_Sargeras), "Doodads\\Cinematic\\TownBurningFireEmitter\\TownBurningFireEmitter.mdl")
        call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Activer_Sargeras), "Doodads\\Cinematic\\TownBurningFireEmitter\\TownBurningFireEmitter.mdl")
        call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(GetRandomLocInRect(gg_rct_Activer_Sargeras), "Doodads\\Cinematic\\TownBurningFireEmitter\\TownBurningFireEmitter.mdl")
        call TriggerSleepAction(1.00)
        call ForForce(GetPlayersAll(), function Trig_Antre_de_Sargeras_Func001Func014A)
        call ShowUnitShow(gg_unit_n086_0240)
        call ShowUnitShow(gg_unit_h0BL_0239)
        call ShowUnitShow(gg_unit_N085_0241)
        call SetUnitOwner(gg_unit_N085_0241, Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), true)
        call AddSpecialEffectTargetUnitBJ("origin", gg_unit_N085_0241, "Doodads\\Cinematic\\TownBurningFireEmitter\\TownBurningFireEmitter.mdl")
        call TriggerSleepAction(3.00)
        call ForForce(GetPlayersAll(), function Trig_Antre_de_Sargeras_Func001Func022A)
        call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAll(), "TRIGSTR_7002")
    else
    endif
endfunction

endfunction

    endif
    return true

endfunction

    call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())

    call ForGroupBJ(udg_GroupUnits, function Trig_Campagne_Appel_Frostmourne_Gardien_2_Func003002)
    call DestroyGroup(udg_GroupUnits)
    call ForceCinematicSubtitlesBJ(true)
    call TransmissionFromUnitWithNameBJ(GetPlayersAll(), gg_unit_nrvd_0526, "TRIGSTR_7956", gg_snd_H09Guardian11, "TRIGSTR_7957", bj_TIMETYPE_ADD, 0.00, true)
    call TransmissionFromUnitWithNameBJ(GetPlayersAll(), GetTriggerUnit(), "TRIGSTR_7958", gg_snd_H09Arthas09, "TRIGSTR_7959", bj_TIMETYPE_ADD, 0.00, true)
    call KillUnit(gg_unit_nrvd_0526)
    call KillDestructable(gg_dest_ZTd3_14859)
    set udg_GroupUnits=GetUnitsInRectAll(gg_rct_Appel_de_Frostmourne_Gardien)
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_GroupUnits, function Trig_Campagne_Appel_Frostmourne_Gardien_2_Func011002)
    call DestroyGroup(udg_GroupUnits)
    call TriggerSleepAction(2)
    call TransmissionFromUnitWithNameBJ(GetPlayersAll(), GetTriggerUnit(), "TRIGSTR_7960", gg_snd_H09Arthas09, "TRIGSTR_7961", bj_TIMETYPE_ADD, 0.00, true)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function Trig_Campagne_Appel_Frostmourne_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'Hart' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Campagne_Appel_Frostmourne_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=0
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=11
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        call SetPlayerAbilityAvailableBJ(false, 'A01Q', udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()])
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    call PauseUnitBJ(true, GetTriggerUnit())
    call SetUnitAnimation(GetTriggerUnit(), "stand channel")
    call ForceCinematicSubtitlesBJ(true)
    call TransmissionFromUnitWithNameBJ(GetPlayersAll(), GetTriggerUnit(), "TRIGSTR_7962", gg_snd_H09Arthas09, "TRIGSTR_7963", bj_TIMETYPE_ADD, 0.00, true)
    call SetUnitAnimation(gg_unit_nfrm_0404, "death")
    call TriggerSleepAction(2)
    call PauseUnitBJ(false, GetTriggerUnit())
    call ResetUnitAnimation(GetTriggerUnit())
    set udg_Nombre=GetHeroLevel(GetTriggerUnit())
    call ReplaceUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'Harf', bj_UNIT_STATE_METHOD_RELATIVE)
    call SetHeroLevelBJ(GetLastReplacedUnitBJ(), udg_Nombre, false)
    call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('I000', GetLastReplacedUnitBJ())
    call PlaySoundBJ(gg_snd_Hint)
    call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAll(), "TRIGSTR_7964")
endfunction

    call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())

    call TransmissionFromUnitWithNameBJ(GetPlayersAll(), GetTriggerUnit(), "TRIGSTR_7965", gg_snd_H09Arthas28a, "TRIGSTR_7966", bj_TIMETYPE_ADD, 0.00, true)
    call TriggerSleepAction(2)
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=0
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=11
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        call SetPlayerAbilityAvailableBJ(false, 'A01P', udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()])
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    set udg_Position=GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Exterieur_Trone_de_Glace)
    call SetUnitPositionLoc(GetTriggerUnit(), udg_Position)
    call PanCameraToTimedLocForPlayer(GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_Position, 0)
    call ReplaceUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'Uear', bj_UNIT_STATE_METHOD_MAXIMUM)
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(4, 'uaco', GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_Position, bj_UNIT_FACING)
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'h02V', GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_Position, bj_UNIT_FACING)
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(4, 'ugho', GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_Position, bj_UNIT_FACING)
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(2, 'uabo', GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_Position, bj_UNIT_FACING)
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(2, 'unec', GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_Position, bj_UNIT_FACING)
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'ufro', GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_Position, bj_UNIT_FACING)
    call RemoveLocation(udg_Position)
    call PlaySoundBJ(gg_snd_Hint)
    call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAll(), "TRIGSTR_7969")
endfunction

function Trig_Campagne_Devenir_Roi_Liche_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())

    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=11
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        call SetPlayerAbilityAvailableBJ(false, 'A01U', udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()])
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    call PauseUnitBJ(true, GetTriggerUnit())
    call SetUnitAnimation(GetTriggerUnit(), "spell")
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=0
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=11
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        call CameraSetEQNoiseForPlayer(udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], 7.00)
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    call TriggerSleepAction(1.00)
    call SetUnitOwner(gg_unit_nzlc_0405, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), true)
    call PauseUnitBJ(false, GetTriggerUnit())
    call ResetUnitAnimation(GetTriggerUnit())
    call ReplaceUnitBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 'U006', bj_UNIT_STATE_METHOD_RELATIVE)
    call UnitAddItemByIdSwapped('I00J', GetLastReplacedUnitBJ())
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=0
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=11
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        call CameraClearNoiseForPlayer(udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()])
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    call PlaySoundBJ(gg_snd_Hint)
    call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAll(), "TRIGSTR_7972")
endfunction

    call TriggerRegisterEnterRectSimple(gg_trg_Campagne_Devenir_Roi_Liche, gg_rct_Campagne_Devenir_Roi_Liche)

        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'BTtc' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetDestructableTypeId(GetEnumDestructable()) == 'BTtw' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

        return false
    endif
    return true

function Trig_Campagne_Scierie_Chanteguerre_Func004A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Campagne_Scierie_Chanteguerre_Func004Func001C() ) then
        call KillDestructable(GetEnumDestructable())
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Campagne_Scierie_Chanteguerre_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=0
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=11
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        call SetPlayerTechMaxAllowedSwap('R01V', 0, udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()])
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
    call PlaySoundBJ(gg_snd_Hint)
    call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAll(), "TRIGSTR_7973")
    call EnumDestructablesInRectAll(gg_rct_Campagne_Scierie_Chanteguerre, function Trig_Campagne_Scierie_Chanteguerre_Func004A)
    call ShowUnitShow(gg_unit_h033_0275)
    call SetUnitOwner(gg_unit_h033_0275, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), true)
    call ForceCinematicSubtitlesBJ(true)
    call TransmissionFromUnitTypeWithNameBJ(GetPlayersAll(), GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), 'Ogrh', "TRIGSTR_7974", GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit()), gg_snd_O04Grom01, "TRIGSTR_7975", bj_TIMETYPE_ADD, 0, true)
endfunction

    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A079' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Faire_pousser_des_arbres_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A081' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Faire_pousser_des_arbres_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_Position=GetSpellTargetLoc()
    if ( Trig_Faire_pousser_des_arbres_Func002C() ) then
        call CreateDestructableLoc('ATtr', udg_Position, GetRandomDirectionDeg(), 1, 0)
    else
        if ( Trig_Faire_pousser_des_arbres_Func002Func001C() ) then
            call CreateDestructableLoc('LTlt', udg_Position, GetRandomDirectionDeg(), 1, 0)
        else
            if ( Trig_Faire_pousser_des_arbres_Func002Func001Func002C() ) then
                call CreateDestructableLoc('CTtr', udg_Position, GetRandomDirectionDeg(), 1, 0)
            else
                if ( Trig_Faire_pousser_des_arbres_Func002Func001Func002Func002C() ) then
                    call CreateDestructableLoc('NTtw', udg_Position, GetRandomDirectionDeg(), 1, 0)
                else
                    if ( Trig_Faire_pousser_des_arbres_Func002Func001Func002Func002Func002C() ) then
                        call CreateDestructableLoc('WTst', udg_Position, GetRandomDirectionDeg(), 1, 0)
                    else
                        if ( Trig_Faire_pousser_des_arbres_Func002Func001Func002Func002Func002Func002C() ) then
                            call CreateDestructableLoc('BTtw', udg_Position, GetRandomDirectionDeg(), 1, 0)
                        else
                            if ( Trig_Faire_pousser_des_arbres_Func002Func001Func002Func002Func002Func002Func002C() ) then
                                call CreateDestructableLoc('OTtw', udg_Position, GetRandomDirectionDeg(), 1, 0)
                            else
                                if ( Trig_Faire_pousser_des_arbres_Func002Func001Func002Func002Func002Func002Func002Func002C() ) then
                                    call CreateDestructableLoc('ZTtw', udg_Position, GetRandomDirectionDeg(), 1, 0)
                                else
                                endif
                            endif
                        endif
                    endif
                endif
            endif
        endif
    endif
    call RemoveLocation(udg_Position)
endfunction
