        call SetUnitScalePercent(GetSpellTargetUnit(), 170.00, 170.00, 170.00)
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
    if ( (GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A04L') ) then // INLINED!!
        call SetUnitScalePercent(GetSpellTargetUnit(), 180.00, 180.00, 180.00)
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
    if ( (GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A04M') ) then // INLINED!!
        call SetUnitScalePercent(GetSpellTargetUnit(), 190.00, 190.00, 190.00)
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Tailles_Unites takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Tailles_Unites=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Tailles_Unites, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_EFFECT)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Tailles_Unites, function Trig_Tailles_Unites_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Stop Faire pousser des arbres
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Stop_Faire_pousser_des_arbres_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'h06M' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Stop_Faire_pousser_des_arbres_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A04T' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Stop_Faire_pousser_des_arbres_Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A04O' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Stop_Faire_pousser_des_arbres_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Stop_Faire_pousser_des_arbres_Func002C() ) then
        call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('A04T', GetTriggerUnit())
        call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A04O', GetTriggerUnit())
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=0
        set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=11
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
            call SetPlayerAbilityAvailableBJ(true, 'A078', udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()])
            set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
        endloop
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=0
        set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=11
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
            call SetPlayerAbilityAvailableBJ(true, 'A045', udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()])
            set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
        endloop
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Stop_Faire_pousser_des_arbres_Func003C() ) then
        call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('A04O', GetTriggerUnit())
        call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A04T', GetTriggerUnit())
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=0
        set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=11
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
            call SetPlayerAbilityAvailableBJ(false, 'A078', udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()])
            set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
        endloop
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=0
        set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=11
        loop
            exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
            call SetPlayerAbilityAvailableBJ(false, 'A045', udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()])
            set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
        endloop
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Stop_Faire_pousser_des_arbres takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Stop_Faire_pousser_des_arbres=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Stop_Faire_pousser_des_arbres, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_EFFECT)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Stop_Faire_pousser_des_arbres, Condition(function Trig_Stop_Faire_pousser_des_arbres_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Stop_Faire_pousser_des_arbres, function Trig_Stop_Faire_pousser_des_arbres_Actions)
endfunction

function Trig_Remove_un_joueur_Func002002002 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( UnitHasBuffBJ(GetFilterUnit(), 'B00Y') == false )
endfunction

function Trig_Remove_un_joueur_Func003A takes nothing returns nothing
    call RemoveUnit(GetEnumUnit())
endfunction

function Trig_Remove_un_joueur_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_Nombre=S2I(SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 9, 10))
    set udg_GroupUnits=GetUnitsOfPlayerMatching(udg_Joueur[( udg_Nombre - 1 )], Condition(function Trig_Remove_un_joueur_Func002002002))
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_GroupUnits, function Trig_Remove_un_joueur_Func003A)
    call DestroyGroup(udg_GroupUnits)
endfunction

//===========================================================================

    if ( not ( GetTriggerPlayer() == udg_Admin ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Appel_du_gardien_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call DisableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())
    call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Fin_du_Gardien)
    call QuestMessageBJ(GetPlayersAll(), bj_QUESTMESSAGE_UPDATED, "TRIGSTR_3575")
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'H06O', udg_Admin, GetRectCenter(gg_rct_Ile_de_Sargeras_Exterieur), bj_UNIT_FACING)
    set udg_Createurdelamap=GetLastCreatedUnit()
    call SetHeroLevelBJ(udg_Createurdelamap, 15, false)
    call SelectHeroSkill(udg_Createurdelamap, 'A05M')
    call SelectHeroSkill(udg_Createurdelamap, 'A05L')
    call SelectHeroSkill(udg_Createurdelamap, 'A05N')
    call SelectHeroSkill(udg_Createurdelamap, 'A058')
    call SelectHeroSkill(udg_Createurdelamap, 'A05P')
endfunction

endfunction

function Trig_Sauver_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_Nombre=S2I(SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 9, 10))
    // Alliance
    if ( (SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 11, 25) == "humain") ) then // INLINED!!
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(5, 'hpea', udg_Joueur[( udg_Nombre - 1 )], udg_SauverPoint[( udg_Nombre - 1 )], bj_UNIT_FACING)
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
    if ( (SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 11, 19) == "nain") ) then // INLINED!!
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(5, 'h01O', udg_Joueur[( udg_Nombre - 1 )], udg_SauverPoint[( udg_Nombre - 1 )], bj_UNIT_FACING)
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
    if ( (SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 11, 25) == "haut elfe") ) then // INLINED!!
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(5, 'n006', udg_Joueur[( udg_Nombre - 1 )], udg_SauverPoint[( udg_Nombre - 1 )], bj_UNIT_FACING)
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
    if ( (SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 11, 19) == "edn") ) then // INLINED!!
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(5, 'ewsp', udg_Joueur[( udg_Nombre - 1 )], udg_SauverPoint[( udg_Nombre - 1 )], bj_UNIT_FACING)
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
    if ( (SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 11, 19) == "worgen") ) then // INLINED!!
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(5, 'h04E', udg_Joueur[( udg_Nombre - 1 )], udg_SauverPoint[( udg_Nombre - 1 )], bj_UNIT_FACING)
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
    if ( (SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 11, 19) == "draenei") ) then // INLINED!!
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(5, 'ndrl', udg_Joueur[( udg_Nombre - 1 )], udg_SauverPoint[( udg_Nombre - 1 )], bj_UNIT_FACING)
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
    if ( (SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 11, 19) == "pandaren") ) then // INLINED!!
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(5, 'h07N', udg_Joueur[( udg_Nombre - 1 )], udg_SauverPoint[( udg_Nombre - 1 )], bj_UNIT_FACING)
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
    // Horde
    if ( (SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 11, 19) == "orc") ) then // INLINED!!
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(5, 'opeo', udg_Joueur[( udg_Nombre - 1 )], udg_SauverPoint[( udg_Nombre - 1 )], bj_UNIT_FACING)
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
    if ( (SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 11, 19) == "tauren") ) then // INLINED!!
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(5, 'o00E', udg_Joueur[( udg_Nombre - 1 )], udg_SauverPoint[( udg_Nombre - 1 )], bj_UNIT_FACING)
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
    if ( (SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 11, 19) == "gobelin") ) then // INLINED!!
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(5, 'o01R', udg_Joueur[( udg_Nombre - 1 )], udg_SauverPoint[( udg_Nombre - 1 )], bj_UNIT_FACING)
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
    if ( (SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 11, 25) == "troll foret") ) then // INLINED!!

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Mode zombie infestation
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Mode_zombie_infestation_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetKillingUnitBJ()) == 'n00K' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Mode_zombie_infestation_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetKillingUnitBJ()) == 'ndmu' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Mode_zombie_infestation_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Mode_zombie_infestation_Func001C() ) then
        set udg_DyingUnitPosition=GetUnitLoc(GetDyingUnit())
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'nzom', GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnitBJ()), udg_DyingUnitPosition, bj_UNIT_FACING)
        call RemoveLocation(udg_DyingUnitPosition)
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Mode_zombie_infestation_Func002C() ) then
        set udg_DyingUnitPosition=GetUnitLoc(GetDyingUnit())
        call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'ndmu', GetOwningPlayer(GetKillingUnitBJ()), udg_DyingUnitPosition, bj_UNIT_FACING)
        call RemoveLocation(udg_DyingUnitPosition)
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Mode_zombie_infestation takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Mode_zombie_infestation=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Mode_zombie_infestation)
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Mode_zombie_infestation, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_DEATH)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Mode_zombie_infestation, function Trig_Mode_zombie_infestation_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Portes des Tenebres
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Portes_des_Tenebres_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetEventPlayerChatString() == "-Porte Ouverte" ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Portes_des_Tenebres_Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetEventPlayerChatString() == "-Porte Ferme" ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Portes_des_Tenebres_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Portes_des_Tenebres_Func001C() ) then
        call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAll(), "TRIGSTR_7931")
        call WaygateActivateBJ(true, gg_unit_n001_0362)
        call SetUnitAnimation(gg_unit_n001_0362, "stand work")
        call WaygateActivateBJ(true, gg_unit_n003_0363)
        call SetUnitAnimation(gg_unit_n003_0363, "stand work")
    else
    endif
    if ( Trig_Portes_des_Tenebres_Func002C() ) then
        call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAll(), "TRIGSTR_7932")
        call WaygateActivateBJ(false, gg_unit_n001_0362)
        call ResetUnitAnimation(gg_unit_n001_0362)
        call WaygateActivateBJ(false, gg_unit_n003_0363)
        call ResetUnitAnimation(gg_unit_n003_0363)
    else
    endif
endfunction

    set gg_trg_Portes_des_Tenebres=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Portes_des_Tenebres, function Trig_Portes_des_Tenebres_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Tourner batiment
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Tourner_batiment_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A00J' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Tourner_batiment_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_Position=GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit())
    set udg_Position2=GetSpellTargetLoc()
    set udg_UnitType=GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit())
    set udg_Vie=GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_LIFE, GetTriggerUnit())
    set udg_Mana=GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_MANA, GetTriggerUnit())
    call RemoveUnit(GetTriggerUnit())
    call CreateNUnitsAtLocFacingLocBJ(1, udg_UnitType, GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_Position, udg_Position2)
    call SetUnitLifeBJ(GetLastCreatedUnit(), udg_Vie)
    call SetUnitManaBJ(GetLastCreatedUnit(), udg_Mana)
    call SelectUnitForPlayerSingle(GetLastCreatedUnit(), GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()))
    call RemoveLocation(udg_Position)
    call RemoveLocation(udg_Position2)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Tourner_batiment takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Tourner_batiment=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Tourner_batiment, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SPELL_EFFECT)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Tourner_batiment, Condition(function Trig_Tourner_batiment_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Tourner_batiment, function Trig_Tourner_batiment_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Commande couleur
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Commande_couleur_Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 10, 30) == udg_Couleur[GetForLoopIndexA()] ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Commande_couleur_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=0
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=23
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        if ( Trig_Commande_couleur_Func001Func001C() ) then
            call SetPlayerColorBJ(GetTriggerPlayer(), udg_CouleurJoueur[GetForLoopIndexA()], true)
        else
        endif
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
endfunction

    set gg_trg_Commande_couleur=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Commande_couleur, function Trig_Commande_couleur_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Commandes passif etc
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Commandes_passif_etc_Func003Func002Func001001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetEventPlayerChatString() == "-passif" )
endfunction

function Trig_Commandes_passif_etc_Func003Func002Func002001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetEventPlayerChatString() == "-hostile" )
endfunction

function Trig_Commandes_passif_etc_Func003Func002Func003C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetEventPlayerChatString() == "-remove" ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Commandes_passif_etc_Func003Func002Func004001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetEventPlayerChatString() == "-kill" )
endfunction

function Trig_Commandes_passif_etc_Func003Func002Func005001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetEventPlayerChatString() == "-explode" )
endfunction

function Trig_Commandes_passif_etc_Func003Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetOwningPlayer(udg_Temp_Unit) == udg_Temp_Player ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( UnitHasBuffBJ(udg_Temp_Unit, 'B00Y') == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Commandes_passif_etc_Func003A takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_Temp_Unit=GetEnumUnit()
    if ( Trig_Commandes_passif_etc_Func003Func002C() ) then
        if ( (GetEventPlayerChatString() == "-passif") ) then // INLINED!!
            call SetUnitOwner(udg_Temp_Unit, Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_PASSIVE), true)
        else
            call DoNothing()
        endif
        if ( (GetEventPlayerChatString() == "-hostile") ) then // INLINED!!
            call SetUnitOwner(udg_Temp_Unit, Player(PLAYER_NEUTRAL_AGGRESSIVE), true)
        else
            call DoNothing()
        endif
        if ( Trig_Commandes_passif_etc_Func003Func002Func003C() ) then
            call UnitRemoveItemFromSlotSwapped(1, udg_Temp_Unit)
            call UnitRemoveItemFromSlotSwapped(2, udg_Temp_Unit)
            call UnitRemoveItemFromSlotSwapped(3, udg_Temp_Unit)
            call UnitRemoveItemFromSlotSwapped(4, udg_Temp_Unit)
            call UnitRemoveItemFromSlotSwapped(5, udg_Temp_Unit)
            call UnitRemoveItemFromSlotSwapped(6, udg_Temp_Unit)
            call RemoveUnit(udg_Temp_Unit)
        else
        endif
        if ( (GetEventPlayerChatString() == "-kill") ) then // INLINED!!
            call KillUnit(udg_Temp_Unit)
        else
            call DoNothing()
        endif
        if ( (GetEventPlayerChatString() == "-explode") ) then // INLINED!!
            call ExplodeUnitBJ(udg_Temp_Unit)
        else
            call DoNothing()
        endif
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Commandes_passif_etc_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_Temp_Player=GetTriggerPlayer()
    set udg_GroupUnits=GetUnitsSelectedAll(udg_Temp_Player)
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_GroupUnits, function Trig_Commandes_passif_etc_Func003A)
    call DestroyGroup(udg_GroupUnits)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Commandes_passif_etc takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Commandes_passif_etc=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Commandes_passif_etc, function Trig_Commandes_passif_etc_Actions)
endfunction

    if ( not ( SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 1, 10) == "-set life " ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Commandes_set_life_and_mana_Func004Func001Func002Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 1, 10) == "-set mana " ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Commandes_set_life_and_mana_Func004Func001Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetOwningPlayer(udg_Temp_Unit) == udg_Temp_Player ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( UnitHasBuffBJ(udg_Temp_Unit, 'B00Y') == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Commandes_set_life_and_mana_Func004Func001A takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_Temp_Unit=GetEnumUnit()
    if ( Trig_Commandes_set_life_and_mana_Func004Func001Func002C() ) then
        if ( Trig_Commandes_set_life_and_mana_Func004Func001Func002Func001C() ) then
            call BlzSetUnitMaxHP(udg_Temp_Unit, udg_Nombre)
            call SetUnitLifePercentBJ(udg_Temp_Unit, 100)
        else
        endif
        if ( Trig_Commandes_set_life_and_mana_Func004Func001Func002Func002C() ) then
            call BlzSetUnitMaxMana(udg_Temp_Unit, udg_Nombre)
            call SetUnitManaPercentBJ(udg_Temp_Unit, 100)
        else
        endif
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Commandes_set_life_and_mana_Func004C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_Nombre >= 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( udg_Nombre <= 500000 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Commandes_set_life_and_mana_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_Temp_Player=GetTriggerPlayer()
    set udg_GroupUnits=GetUnitsSelectedAll(udg_Temp_Player)
    set udg_Nombre=S2I(SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 11, 19))
    if ( Trig_Commandes_set_life_and_mana_Func004C() ) then
        call ForGroupBJ(udg_GroupUnits, function Trig_Commandes_set_life_and_mana_Func004Func001A)
        call DestroyGroup(udg_GroupUnits)
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Commande set damage
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Commande_set_damage_Func004Func001Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetOwningPlayer(udg_Temp_Unit) == udg_Temp_Player ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( UnitHasBuffBJ(udg_Temp_Unit, 'B00Y') == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 1, 12) == "-set damage " ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Commande_set_damage_Func004Func001A takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_Temp_Unit=GetEnumUnit()
    if ( Trig_Commande_set_damage_Func004Func001Func002C() ) then
        call BlzSetUnitBaseDamage(udg_Temp_Unit, udg_Nombre, 1)
        call BlzSetUnitBaseDamage(udg_Temp_Unit, udg_Nombre, 2)
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Commande_set_damage_Func004C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_Nombre >= 1 ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Commande_set_damage_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_Temp_Player=GetTriggerPlayer()
    set udg_GroupUnits=GetUnitsSelectedAll(udg_Temp_Player)
    set udg_Nombre=S2I(SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 13, 19))
    if ( Trig_Commande_set_damage_Func004C() ) then
        call ForGroupBJ(udg_GroupUnits, function Trig_Commande_set_damage_Func004Func001A)
    else
    endif
    call DestroyGroup(udg_GroupUnits)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Commande_set_damage takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Commande_set_damage=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Commande_set_damage, function Trig_Commande_set_damage_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Commande wood and gold
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Commande_wood_and_gold_Func002001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 1, 6) == "-wood " )
endfunction

function Trig_Commande_wood_and_gold_Func003001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 1, 6) == "-gold " )
endfunction

function Trig_Commande_wood_and_gold_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_Nombre=S2I(SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 7, 19))
    if ( (SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 1, 6) == "-wood ") ) then // INLINED!!
        call AdjustPlayerStateBJ(udg_Nombre, GetTriggerPlayer(), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_LUMBER)
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
    if ( (SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 1, 6) == "-gold ") ) then // INLINED!!
        call AdjustPlayerStateBJ(udg_Nombre, GetTriggerPlayer(), PLAYER_STATE_RESOURCE_GOLD)
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
endfunction

    set gg_trg_Commande_wood_and_gold=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Commande_wood_and_gold, function Trig_Commande_wood_and_gold_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Commande set name and heroname
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Commande_set_name_and_heroname_Func001001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 1, 10) == "-set name " )
endfunction

function Trig_Commande_set_name_and_heroname_Func002001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 1, 16) == "-set heros name " )
endfunction

function Trig_Commande_set_name_and_heroname_Func005Func001Func002Func001001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 1, 10) == "-set name " )
endfunction

function Trig_Commande_set_name_and_heroname_Func005Func001Func002Func002001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 1, 16) == "-set heros name " )
endfunction

function Trig_Commande_set_name_and_heroname_Func005Func001Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetOwningPlayer(udg_Temp_Unit) == udg_Temp_Player ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( UnitHasBuffBJ(udg_Temp_Unit, 'B00Y') == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Commande_set_name_and_heroname_Func005Func001A takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_Temp_Unit=GetEnumUnit()
    if ( Trig_Commande_set_name_and_heroname_Func005Func001Func002C() ) then
        if ( (SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 1, 10) == "-set name ") ) then // INLINED!!
            call BlzSetUnitName(udg_Temp_Unit, udg_Chaine)
        else
            call DoNothing()
        endif
        if ( (SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 1, 16) == "-set heros name ") ) then // INLINED!!
            call BlzSetHeroProperName(udg_Temp_Unit, udg_Chaine)
        else
            call DoNothing()
        endif
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Commande_set_name_and_heroname_Func005C takes nothing returns boolean
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Commande_set_name_and_heroname_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( (SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 1, 10) == "-set name ") ) then // INLINED!!
        set udg_Chaine=SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 11, 35)
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
    if ( (SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 1, 16) == "-set heros name ") ) then // INLINED!!
        set udg_Chaine=SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 17, 45)
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
    set udg_Temp_Player=GetTriggerPlayer()
    set udg_GroupUnits=GetUnitsSelectedAll(udg_Temp_Player)
    if ( (true) ) then // INLINED!!
        call ForGroupBJ(udg_GroupUnits, function Trig_Commande_set_name_and_heroname_Func005Func001A)
    else
    endif
    call DestroyGroup(udg_GroupUnits)
endfunction

    set gg_trg_Commande_set_name_and_heroname=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Commande_set_name_and_heroname, function Trig_Commande_set_name_and_heroname_Actions)
endfunction

endfunction

        return false

    if ( not ( UnitHasBuffBJ(udg_Temp_Unit, 'B00Y') == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif

        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Commande unite couleur
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Commande_unite_couleur_Func001Func001Func003Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( udg_Temp_Player == GetOwningPlayer(udg_Temp_Unit) ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Commande_unite_couleur_Func001Func001Func003A takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_Temp_Unit=GetEnumUnit()
    if ( Trig_Commande_unite_couleur_Func001Func001Func003Func002C() ) then
        call SetUnitColor(udg_Temp_Unit, GetPlayerColor(udg_Joueur[GetForLoopIndexA()]))
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Commande_unite_couleur_Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( SubStringBJ(GetEventPlayerChatString(), 8, 20) == udg_Couleur[GetForLoopIndexA()] ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Commande_unite_couleur_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set bj_forLoopAIndex=0
    set bj_forLoopAIndexEnd=23
    loop
        exitwhen bj_forLoopAIndex > bj_forLoopAIndexEnd
        if ( Trig_Commande_unite_couleur_Func001Func001C() ) then
            set udg_Temp_Player=GetTriggerPlayer()
            set udg_GroupUnits=GetUnitsSelectedAll(udg_Temp_Player)
            call ForGroupBJ(udg_GroupUnits, function Trig_Commande_unite_couleur_Func001Func001Func003A)
            call DestroyGroup(udg_GroupUnits)
        else
        endif
        set bj_forLoopAIndex=bj_forLoopAIndex + 1
    endloop
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Commande_unite_couleur takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Commande_unite_couleur=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Commande_unite_couleur, function Trig_Commande_unite_couleur_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Commmande statue
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Commmande_statue_Func003Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitPausedBJ(udg_Temp_Unit) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Commmande_statue_Func003Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetOwningPlayer(udg_Temp_Unit) == udg_Temp_Player ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( UnitHasBuffBJ(udg_Temp_Unit, 'B00Y') == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Commmande_statue_Func003A takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_Temp_Unit=GetEnumUnit()
    if ( Trig_Commmande_statue_Func003Func002C() ) then
        if ( Trig_Commmande_statue_Func003Func002Func001C() ) then
            call PauseUnitBJ(false, udg_Temp_Unit)
            call SetUnitColor(udg_Temp_Unit, GetPlayerColor(GetOwningPlayer(udg_Temp_Unit)))
            call BlzSetUnitName(udg_Temp_Unit, UnitId2StringBJ(GetUnitTypeId(udg_Temp_Unit)))
            call SetUnitTimeScalePercent(udg_Temp_Unit, 100.00)
            call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('A07Z', udg_Temp_Unit)
            call UnitWakeUpBJ(udg_Temp_Unit)
        else
            call PauseUnitBJ(true, udg_Temp_Unit)
            call SetUnitColor(udg_Temp_Unit, ConvertPlayerColor(24))
            call BlzSetUnitName(udg_Temp_Unit, ( "Statue de " + UnitId2StringBJ(GetUnitTypeId(udg_Temp_Unit)) ))
            call SetUnitTimeScalePercent(udg_Temp_Unit, 0.00)
        endif
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Commmande_statue_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_Temp_Player=GetTriggerPlayer()
    set udg_GroupUnits=GetUnitsSelectedAll(udg_Temp_Player)
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_GroupUnits, function Trig_Commmande_statue_Func003A)
    call DestroyGroup(udg_GroupUnits)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Commmande_statue takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Commmande_statue=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Commmande_statue, function Trig_Commmande_statue_Actions)
endfunction

    endif
    return true

        return false
    endif

        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

    set udg_Temp_Unit=GetEnumUnit()
    if ( Trig_Commmande_collision_Func003Func002C() ) then
        if ( Trig_Commmande_collision_Func003Func002Func001C() ) then
            call SetUnitPathing(udg_Temp_Unit, false)
        else
            call SetUnitPathing(udg_Temp_Unit, true)
        endif
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Commande dormir
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Commande_dormir_Func003Func002Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( SubStringBJ(GetUnitName(udg_Temp_Unit), 1, 10) != "statue de " ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Commande_dormir_Func003Func002Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitPausedBJ(udg_Temp_Unit) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( SubStringBJ(GetUnitName(udg_Temp_Unit), 1, 10) != "statue de " ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Commande_dormir_Func003Func002C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetOwningPlayer(udg_Temp_Unit) == udg_Temp_Player ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( UnitHasBuffBJ(udg_Temp_Unit, 'B00Y') == false ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Commande_dormir_Func003A takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_Temp_Unit=GetEnumUnit()
    if ( Trig_Commande_dormir_Func003Func002C() ) then
        if ( Trig_Commande_dormir_Func003Func002Func001C() ) then
            call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('A07Z', udg_Temp_Unit)
            call PauseUnitBJ(false, udg_Temp_Unit)
            call UnitWakeUpBJ(udg_Temp_Unit)
        else
            if ( Trig_Commande_dormir_Func003Func002Func001Func001C() ) then
                call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A07Z', udg_Temp_Unit)
                call PauseUnitBJ(true, udg_Temp_Unit)
                call UnitAddSleepPerm(udg_Temp_Unit, true)
            else
            endif
        endif
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Commande_dormir_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_Temp_Player=GetTriggerPlayer()
    set udg_GroupUnits=GetUnitsSelectedAll(udg_Temp_Player)
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_GroupUnits, function Trig_Commande_dormir_Func003A)
    call DestroyGroup(udg_GroupUnits)
endfunction

    set gg_trg_Commande_dormir=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Commande_dormir, function Trig_Commande_dormir_Actions)
endfunction

function Trig_reveiller_quand_attaquer_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( IsUnitPausedBJ(GetTriggerUnit()) == true ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    if ( not ( SubStringBJ(GetUnitName(GetTriggerUnit()), 1, 10) != "statue de " ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_reveiller_quand_attaquer_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call PauseUnitBJ(false, GetTriggerUnit())
    call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('A07Z', GetTriggerUnit())
endfunction

    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_reveiller_quand_attaquer, function Trig_reveiller_quand_attaquer_Actions)
endfunction

function Trig_Commande_effets_on_etc_Func003A takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_Temp_Unit=GetEnumUnit()
    if ( Trig_Commande_effets_on_etc_Func003Func002C() ) then
        if ( Trig_Commande_effets_on_etc_Func003Func002Func001C() ) then
            call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A07X', udg_Temp_Unit)
        else
        endif
        if ( Trig_Commande_effets_on_etc_Func003Func002Func002C() ) then
            call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A07W', udg_Temp_Unit)
        else
        endif
        if ( Trig_Commande_effets_on_etc_Func003Func002Func003C() ) then
            call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A07V', udg_Temp_Unit)
        else
        endif
        if ( Trig_Commande_effets_on_etc_Func003Func002Func004C() ) then
            call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A07U', udg_Temp_Unit)
        else
        endif
        if ( Trig_Commande_effets_on_etc_Func003Func002Func005C() ) then
            call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A08E', udg_Temp_Unit)
        else
        endif
        if ( Trig_Commande_effets_on_etc_Func003Func002Func006C() ) then
            call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A07T', udg_Temp_Unit)
            call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A089', udg_Temp_Unit)
            call SetUnitColor(udg_Temp_Unit, GetPlayerColor(GetOwningPlayer(udg_Temp_Unit)))
        else
        endif
        if ( Trig_Commande_effets_on_etc_Func003Func002Func007C() ) then
            call UnitAddAbilityBJ('A07Y', udg_Temp_Unit)
        else
        endif
    else
    endif
endfunction

    set udg_Temp_Player=GetTriggerPlayer()
    set udg_GroupUnits=GetUnitsSelectedAll(udg_Temp_Player)
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_GroupUnits, function Trig_Commande_effets_on_etc_Func003A)
    call DestroyGroup(udg_GroupUnits)
endfunction

    return true

    call EnableTrigger(GetTriggeringTrigger())

    call UnitRemoveAbilityBJ('A05R', gg_unit_h079_0030)

    call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Shield01Damage)
    call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Shield01Enter)
    call EnableTrigger(gg_trg_Shield01Exit)
    call DisplayTextToForce(GetPlayersAll(), "TRIGSTR_3718")

endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Shield01Enter
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Shield01Enter_Func001001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( RACE_UNDEAD == GetUnitRace(GetEnteringUnit()) )
endfunction

function Trig_Shield01Enter_Func001002 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( IsUnitType(GetEnteringUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_UNDEAD) == true )
endfunction

function Trig_Shield01Enter_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not GetBooleanOr((RACE_UNDEAD == GetUnitRace(GetEnteringUnit())), (IsUnitType(GetEnteringUnit(), UNIT_TYPE_UNDEAD) == true)) ) then // INLINED!!
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Shield01Enter_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call GroupAddUnitSimple(GetEnteringUnit(), udg_Shield01Group)
    call SetUnitVertexColorBJ(GetTriggerUnit(), 100, 50.00, 100, 0)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Shield01Enter takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Shield01Enter=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Shield01Enter)
    call TriggerRegisterEnterRectSimple(gg_trg_Shield01Enter, gg_rct_Bouclier_antimv_de_Dalaran)
    call TriggerRegisterEnterRectSimple(gg_trg_Shield01Enter, gg_rct_Bouclier_antimv_de_Dalaran_2)
    call TriggerRegisterEnterRectSimple(gg_trg_Shield01Enter, gg_rct_Bouclier_antimv_de_Dalaran_3)
    call TriggerRegisterEnterRectSimple(gg_trg_Shield01Enter, gg_rct_Bouclier_antimv_de_Dalaran_4)
    call TriggerRegisterEnterRectSimple(gg_trg_Shield01Enter, gg_rct_Bouclier_antimv_de_Dalaran_5)
    call TriggerRegisterEnterRectSimple(gg_trg_Shield01Enter, gg_rct_Bouclier_antimv_de_Dalaran_6)
    call TriggerRegisterEnterRectSimple(gg_trg_Shield01Enter, gg_rct_Bouclier_antimv_de_Dalaran_7)
    call TriggerRegisterEnterRectSimple(gg_trg_Shield01Enter, gg_rct_Bouclier_antimv_de_Dalaran_8)
    call TriggerRegisterEnterRectSimple(gg_trg_Shield01Enter, gg_rct_Bouclier_antimv_de_Dalaran_9)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Shield01Enter, Condition(function Trig_Shield01Enter_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Shield01Enter, function Trig_Shield01Enter_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Shield01Exit
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Shield01Exit_Func001Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( RectContainsUnit(gg_rct_Bouclier_antimv_de_Dalaran, GetEnumUnit()) == false ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( RectContainsUnit(gg_rct_Bouclier_antimv_de_Dalaran_2, GetEnumUnit()) == false ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( RectContainsUnit(gg_rct_Bouclier_antimv_de_Dalaran_3, GetEnumUnit()) == false ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( RectContainsUnit(gg_rct_Bouclier_antimv_de_Dalaran_4, GetEnumUnit()) == false ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( RectContainsUnit(gg_rct_Bouclier_antimv_de_Dalaran_5, GetEnumUnit()) == false ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( RectContainsUnit(gg_rct_Bouclier_antimv_de_Dalaran_6, GetEnumUnit()) == false ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( RectContainsUnit(gg_rct_Bouclier_antimv_de_Dalaran_7, GetEnumUnit()) == false ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( RectContainsUnit(gg_rct_Bouclier_antimv_de_Dalaran_8, GetEnumUnit()) == false ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( RectContainsUnit(gg_rct_Bouclier_antimv_de_Dalaran_9, GetEnumUnit()) == false ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Shield01Exit_Func001Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not Trig_Shield01Exit_Func001Func001Func001C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Shield01Exit_Func001A takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( Trig_Shield01Exit_Func001Func001C() ) then
        call SetUnitVertexColorBJ(GetEnumUnit(), 100, 100, 100, 0)
        call GroupRemoveUnitSimple(GetEnumUnit(), udg_Shield01Group)
    else
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Shield01Exit_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_Shield01Group, function Trig_Shield01Exit_Func001A)
endfunction

    set gg_trg_Shield01Exit=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Shield01Exit)
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventPeriodic(gg_trg_Shield01Exit, 2)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Shield01Exit, function Trig_Shield01Exit_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Shield01Damage
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Shield01Damage_Func001002001001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_LIFE, GetEnumUnit()) > 0.00 )
endfunction

function Trig_Shield01Damage_Func001002001002 takes nothing returns boolean
    return ( GetUnitRace(GetEnumUnit()) == RACE_UNDEAD )
endfunction

function Trig_Shield01Damage_Func001002001 takes nothing returns boolean
    return GetBooleanAnd((GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_LIFE, GetEnumUnit()) > 0.00), (GetUnitRace(GetEnumUnit()) == RACE_UNDEAD)) // INLINED!!
endfunction

function Trig_Shield01Damage_Func001002 takes nothing returns nothing
    if ( (GetBooleanAnd((GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_LIFE, GetEnumUnit()) > 0.00), (GetUnitRace(GetEnumUnit()) == RACE_UNDEAD))) ) then // INLINED!!
        call SetUnitLifeBJ(GetEnumUnit(), ( GetUnitStateSwap(UNIT_STATE_LIFE, GetEnumUnit()) - 15.00 ))
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
endfunction

function Trig_Shield01Damage_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    call ForGroupBJ(udg_Shield01Group, function Trig_Shield01Damage_Func001002)
endfunction

    set gg_trg_Shield01Damage=CreateTrigger()
    call DisableTrigger(gg_trg_Shield01Damage)
    call TriggerRegisterTimerEventPeriodic(gg_trg_Shield01Damage, 1.00)
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Shield01Damage, function Trig_Shield01Damage_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Command 1
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Command_1_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetSummonedUnit()) == 'o03H' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetSummonedUnit()) == 'o03I' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Command_1_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not Trig_Command_1_Func001C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Command_1_Func005C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetSummonedUnit()) == 'o03H' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Command_1_Func006C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetSummonedUnit()) == 'o03I' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Command_1_Func008C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetUnitTypeId(GetSummonedUnit()) == 'o03I' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Command_1_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(GetSummonedUnit())
    call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(udg_TempPoint, "Objects\\Spawnmodels\\Other\\ToonBoom\\ToonBoom.mdl")
    call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
    if ( Trig_Command_1_Func005C() ) then
        call SetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A07J', GetSummonedUnit(), GetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A07K', GetSummoningUnit()))
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
    if ( Trig_Command_1_Func006C() ) then
        call SetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A07J', GetSummonedUnit(), GetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A07I', GetSummoningUnit()))
        call SetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A07L', GetSummonedUnit(), GetUnitAbilityLevelSwapped('A07I', GetSummoningUnit()))
    else
        call DoNothing()
    endif
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    if ( Trig_Command_1_Func008C() ) then
        call SetUnitAnimation(GetSummonedUnit(), "stand")
    else
    endif
endfunction

//===========================================================================
function InitTrig_Command_1 takes nothing returns nothing
    set gg_trg_Command_1=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Command_1, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_SUMMON)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Command_1, Condition(function Trig_Command_1_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Command_1, function Trig_Command_1_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Command 2
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Command_2_Func001C takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'o03I' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    if ( ( GetUnitTypeId(GetTriggerUnit()) == 'o03H' ) ) then
        return true
    endif
    return false
endfunction

function Trig_Command_2_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not Trig_Command_2_Func001C() ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Command_2_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_TempPoint=GetUnitLoc(GetSummonedUnit())
    call AddSpecialEffectLocBJ(GetUnitLoc(GetTriggerUnit()), "Objects\\Spawnmodels\\Other\\ToonBoom\\ToonBoom.mdl")
    call DestroyEffectBJ(GetLastCreatedEffectBJ())
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
endfunction

    set gg_trg_Command_2=CreateTrigger()
    call TriggerRegisterAnyUnitEventBJ(gg_trg_Command_2, EVENT_PLAYER_UNIT_DEATH)
    call TriggerAddCondition(gg_trg_Command_2, Condition(function Trig_Command_2_Conditions))
    call TriggerAddAction(gg_trg_Command_2, function Trig_Command_2_Actions)
endfunction

//===========================================================================
// Trigger: Artillery Strike 1
//===========================================================================
function Trig_Artillery_Strike_1_Conditions takes nothing returns boolean
    if ( not ( GetSpellAbilityId() == 'A07N' ) ) then
        return false
    endif
    return true
endfunction

function Trig_Artillery_Strike_1_Actions takes nothing returns nothing
    set udg_TempPoint=GetSpellTargetLoc()
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'h0BK', GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
    call UnitApplyTimedLifeBJ(3.00, 'BTLF', GetLastCreatedUnit())
    call CreateNUnitsAtLoc(1, 'h0BJ', GetOwningPlayer(GetTriggerUnit()), udg_TempPoint, bj_UNIT_FACING)
    call IssuePointOrderLocBJ(GetLastCreatedUnit(), "clusterrockets", udg_TempPoint)
    call UnitApplyTimedLifeBJ(5.00, 'BTLF', GetLastCreatedUnit())
    call RemoveLocation(udg_TempPoint)
    call TriggerSleepAction(0.50)
    call ResetUnitAnimation(GetTriggerUnit())
endfunction

endfunction
